==================================================================      
=============== STARTING W --> mu + nu ANALYZER    ===============      
==================================================================      
  This package will count the number of muons in the signal space       
define by the user and save these muons to an output file for           
later use. Control kinematic histograms -- provided by the user --      
are also generated and stored in the output file                        
                                                                        
  Provide as an arguments to this macro:                                
1) Period (A,B,AB) 2) Subtract Background (Y/N) 3) Correct Yields (Y/N) 
==================================================================
